## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: nonlinear dynamics / classical mechanics
**Analysis**: This task models the acceleration of a nonlinear harmonic oscillator, where dv_dt depends on position x (restoring force), velocity v (damping), and possibly time t (external driving). The relationship encodes the equation of motion with nonlinear force and/or damping terms.

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Linear harmonic oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x (simple restoring force)
- Duffing oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 (cubic nonlinear restoring force)
- Duffing with quintic: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * x**5 (higher-order nonlinear restoring force)
- Damped linear oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v (restoring force with linear damping)
- Damped Duffing oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * v (Duffing with linear damping)
- Driven damped oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v + c2 * cos(c3 * t) (forced oscillation)
- Van der Pol oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * (1 - x**2) * v + c1 * x (nonlinear damping depending on position)
- Rayleigh oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * v + c1 * v**3 + c2 * x (velocity-dependent nonlinear damping)
- Driven Duffing: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * v + c3 * sin(c4 * t) (driven nonlinear oscillator)
- Mathieu-type parametric: dv_dt = (c0 + c1 * cos(c2 * t)) * x (parametric excitation)
- Softening spring: dv_dt = c0 * x * (1 + c1 * x**2)**(-1) (rational restoring force with softening)
- Nonlinear damping with quadratic velocity: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v * abs(v) (quadratic velocity damping)
- Coupled position-velocity nonlinearity: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**2 * v (position-dependent damping)
- Pendulum-like: dv_dt = c0 * sin(c1 * x) (sinusoidal restoring force from pendulum dynamics)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope ã Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects ã Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay ã Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior ã Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects ã Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Odd-power restoring forces (x, xô°, xãç) ã symmetric potential wells preserving oscillation symmetry
- Velocity-dependent terms proportional to v ã energy dissipation or injection (damping/driving)
- Position-velocity product terms like xôýôñv ã amplitude-dependent damping (self-excited oscillations, limit cycles)
- Sinusoidal time dependence sin(côñt) or cos(côñt) ã external periodic driving force
- Cubic position term xô° with opposite sign to linear term ã Duffing-type hardening or softening spring nonlinearity
- Terms like (1 - xôý)ôñv ã Van der Pol type self-limiting oscillation with amplitude-dependent energy balance
- Even powers of x multiplying v ã nonlinear damping that breaks time-reversal symmetry while preserving spatial symmetry
- Parametric modulation (time-dependent coefficient on x) ã parametric resonance and instability phenomena
